\"arangod/RocksDBEngine/RocksDBCollection.h\",\n      \"symbol\": \"RocksDBCollection\"\n    }\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"The AQL query execution pipeline in ArangoDB is orchestrated through several key C++ components:\\n\\n1. **Query Entry Point** (arangod/Aql/Query.h, Query class): The Query class is the main entry point for AQL query execution. It inherits from QueryContext and manages the entire lifecycle of a query, including parsing, optimization, and execution.\\n\\n2. **Parsing Phase** (arangod/Aql/Parser.cpp/.h, Parser class): The Parser class implements the AQL query parser. It takes a query string and transforms it into an Abstract Syntax Tree (AST). The parser is initialized with QueryContext, Ast, and QueryString references, and provides methods like parse() and parseWithDetails() to process AQL queries.\\n\\n3. **Execution Plan Creation** (arangod/Aql/ExecutionPlan.cpp/.h, ExecutionPlan class): The ExecutionPlan class represents the initial query plan created from the AST. It contains methods like instantiateFromAst() to construct a plan from the AST, and manages execution nodes that form the basis for the execution strategy.\\n\\n4. **Query Optimization** (arangod/Aql/Optimizer.cpp/.h, Optimizer class): The Optimizer class transforms the initial execution plan through a series of optimization rules. It uses a PlanList to manage multiple candidate plans and iteratively applies optimizer rules to improve query performance. The Optimizer works with OptimizerRules to transform and optimize ExecutionPlans.\\n\\n5. **Execution Engine** (arangod/Aql/ExecutionEngine.cpp/.h, ExecutionEngine class): The ExecutionEngine is responsible for instantiating and managing the execution of the optimized plan. It creates ExecutionBlocks from the optimized ExecutionPlan via createBlocks() method. The ExecutionEngine manages the root block and coordinates the execution pipeline using AqlItemBlockManager for memory management.\\n\\n6. **Execution Blocks** (arangod/Aql/ExecutionBlock.cpp/.h, ExecutionBlock class): ExecutionBlock is the base class for all execution nodes. Each block represents a stage in the query pipeline (e.g., collection scan, filtering, sorting, aggregation). Blocks implement the execute() method with cursor management via initializeCursor() and implement methods for data processing through getSome() and skipSome() methods.\\n\\n7. **Transaction Management** (arangod/Transaction/Methods.cpp/.h, Methods class): The Methods class provides the transaction interface for executing operations. It manages transaction context, locks, and coordinates with the storage engine. Methods handles various DML operations like reads and writes with proper isolation levels.\\n\\n8. **Transaction Coordination** (arangod/Transaction/Manager.cpp/.h, Manager class): The Manager class tracks and manages TransactionState instances. It uses a PlanList to manage multiple candidate plans and iteratively applies optimizer rules to improve query performance. The Optimizer works with OptimizerRules to transform and optimize ExecutionPlans.\\n\\n5. **Execution Engine** (arangod/Aql/ExecutionEngine.cpp/.h, ExecutionEngine class): The ExecutionEngine is responsible for instantiating and managing the execution of the optimized plan.
